msg:I am a Ctrip Black Diamond member and I often book hotels through Ctrip due to work reasons. This year, I decided to record my hotel stay experience and share it with my friends online. I also did my own consumption without reimbursement or third-party sponsorship to ensure an independent and fair description:

üéÅ Reasons for staying at Park Hyatt:
üçÄNear the Mixc City, the core shopping area of Qianjiang New Town; although I personally prefer Diaoyutai (high cost performance), I have never stayed at Park Hyatt Hangzhou before and wanted to take my family to experience it, so I booked it for three days.

üéÅCheck-in period 2022/2/12-2022/2/15
üçÄIt is necessary to specify the time of the check-in experience to let everyone know that the people or things I found in this hotel only represent this stage. Maybe a year later, these employees will leave or some problems will be solved. It didn't mean forever üòÄ

Hotel advantages:
üßßThe geographical location is very advantageous. Qianjiang New Town is a new financial center and an emerging shopping center in Hangzhou (I personally think that the Mixc City has replaced the Hangzhou Tower). Compared with the other two nearby luxury hotels, Conrad and Diaoyutai, go to It is very convenient for shopping and dining in Vientiane City. Turn left in the lobby of Park Hyatt Hotel and get off the elevator, which leads directly to Vientiane City B1. Haha, even if it is windy and rainy outside, you don‚Äôt need to bring an umbrella. I can go back to my room immediately. On the 37th floor of the dining hotel, there is a black pearl restaurant, Yuexuan Chinese restaurant, which you can try. The price per person is around 800-1000, but it is basically okay to not step on thunder. If you can't book a seat, call the guest service "complaint" and say that the in-house guests can't eat... Basically it can be arranged üòú
üßßThe hotel's hardware facilities are good and well maintained! It is estimated that it has something to do with the management focus of the management team. Facility maintenance and cleaning are the first, and the second is to solve customer problems. It is responsible for the owner and shareholders. If the hardware facilities are broken, they will be abandoned by customers. There is a probability that the software service will not be good at least, but it will not work. Just apologize! The above is just a joke, it shows that the leadership of Park Hyatt Hotel is smart! When it is not possible to cover everything, at least distinguish the importance and urgency. The decoration details of the room are very delicate, the background of the bed is a patterned light mapping, the glass in the bathroom should have an anti-fog area if I read it correctly, the electric curtains are flexible and intact, and the telephone is intact... The hotel has been in place for 5 years, and the hardware facilities are in good condition! The places that need to be suggested are the electric windows and doors and the TV. Once people leave the room, they will be closed immediately, and when they come back, they have to start again, which will waste some time
Unfortunately, the hardware
‚Äº Ô∏èThe beds in Park Hyatt Hotel are too soft... Friends with bad waists should not stay here. After discovering this on the first day, it was suggested by the front desk of the hotel, and the answer was that all the beds are so soft... If you want to get me a block I have no choice but to accept the hard board. After all, the money has been paid, so I can't refund it... There are only two possibilities for this situation: 1. Hangzhou Park Hyatt only considers some young customers when purchasing beds, because they may prefer softer beds. Well, for example, the couple's water bed in the past; 2, these beds have been collapsed for 5 years... Then the hotel management has not replaced them in order to save money.

hotel services
üßßThe hotel's food and beverage department (breakfast), front desk, and guest rooms are all very hygienic. During this epidemic, I saw a group of young people (should be new recruits) in Park Hyatt Hangzhou may be a little ****y or flawed in terms of service, but it was definitely not intentional , and always maintain the humble learning and hard-working work style of newcomers. I believe that if I can infect guests like me, at least I will be tolerant to them, yes! Tolerance and understanding are important! Everyone is in a good mood!
The unfortunate thing about the service is
‚Äº Ô∏èThe waiter who checks in and out of the building in the lobby on the first floor is a bit rigid, and unpleasant happened twice in three days. I went back to my room after shopping from the mall in three days. My family has already scanned the code. Two days of them, the rigid waiter said that they must ask me Scan the code, I said that I am a guest of the hotel, and I have things in both hands. My relatives have already scanned it, so I don‚Äôt need to scan it. I still argue with me, and I finally have no choice but to say which room I am in. Come to the room and find me! It didn't come after that! But the waiter on one of the days was very warm-hearted. At the beginning, he said to scan the code, but when he saw my shopping items in both hands, he immediately said that it was okay if it was not convenient to scan, and he took the initiative to help me press the elevator... I don't know if it was An apprentice taught by a master? People are still smart and rigid! Hope to improve

The above is my stay experience at Park Hyatt Hangzhou, I hope it will be useful to you
